function buildProcessTime(dJavaScriptStart, sPHPProcessTime)
{
  var dJavaScriptEnd, dSecond, sAfter, sProcess;

  dJavaScriptEnd = new Date() - 0;
  dSecond = Math.floor((dJavaScriptEnd - dJavaScriptStart) / 1000);
  dAfter = (dJavaScriptEnd - dJavaScriptStart) % 1000;
  if      (dAfter < 10 ) { sAfter = '.00' + dAfter; }
  else if (dAfter < 100) { sAfter = '.0'  + dAfter; }
  else                   { sAfter = '.'   + dAfter; }
  sProcess = dSecond + sAfter;
  
  return 'ProcessTime [PHP]' + sPHPProcessTime + ' [JS]' + sProcess;
}

function getURLParameter()
{
  var i, ssParameter, sQuery, dsQuery, dsKeyValue;

  ssParameter = new Array();

  sQuery = location.search;
  if (sQuery == '') {
    return ssParameter;
  }
  
  dsQuery = sQuery.replace( '?' , '' ).split( '&' );
  for (i = 0; i < dsQuery.length; i++) {
    dsKeyValue = dsQuery[i].split( '=' );
    ssParameter[ dsKeyValue[0] ] = dsKeyValue[1];
  }

  return ssParameter;
}

/**
 * Hash：二次元配列ソートのクラス.
 */
function Hash(_sKey, _dValue)
{
  this.sKey   = _sKey;
  this.dValue = _dValue;
}
function sortHash(dhHash)
{
  function quicksortHash(start, end)
  {
    var n;
    var x = dhHash[Math.floor((start + end) / 2)].dValue;
    var i = start;
    var j = end;
  
    while (true) {
      while (dhHash[i].dValue < x) {
        i++;
      }
      while (x < dhHash[j].dValue) {
        j--;
      }
      if (j <= i) {
        break;
      }
      n = dhHash[i];
      dhHash[i] = dhHash[j];
      dhHash[j] = n;
      i++;
      j--; 
    }
    if (start < i - 1) {
      quicksortHash(start, i - 1);
    }
    if (j + 1 < end) {
      quicksortHash(j + 1, end);
    }
  }

  quicksortHash(0, dhHash.length - 1);

  return dhHash;
}

/**
 * 入力配列を昇順ソートするためのキー配列を取得.
 * @param   配列
 * @return  昇順ソートのためのキー配列
 */
function createAscKeys(dsArray)
{
  var i, dhHash, ddSort;
  
  if (dsArray.length == 0) {
    return new Array();
  }
  
  dhHash = new Array();
  for (i = 0; i < dsArray.length; i++) {
    dhHash[i] = new Hash(i, dsArray[i]);
  }
  dhHash = sortHash(dhHash);
  ddSort = new Array();
  for (i = 0; i < dsArray.length; i++) {
    ddSort[i] = dhHash[i].sKey - 0;
  }
  
  return ddSort;
}

/**
 * 入力配列を降順ソートするためのキー配列を取得.
 * @param   配列
 * @return  降順ソートのためのキー配列
 */
function createDescKeys(dsArray)
{
  var i, dhHash, ddSort;
  
  if (dsArray.length == 0) {
    return new Array();
  }
  
  dhHash = new Array();
  for (i = 0; i < dsArray.length; i++) {
    dhHash[i] = new Hash(i, dsArray[i]);
  }
  dhHash = sortHash(dhHash);
  ddSort = new Array();
  for (i = 0; i < dsArray.length; i++) {
    ddSort[i] = dhHash[dsArray.length - 1 - i].sKey - 0;
  }
  
  return ddSort;
}

/**
 * 入力の数値配列のRankを取得.
 * @param  数値配列
 * @param  降順ソートのためのキー配列
 * @return  数値配列に対応するRank
 */
function createRank(ddArray, ddDescKeys) {
  var ddRank, dUpperPoint, dUpperRank, i;
  
  ddRank = new Array();
  dUpperPoint = 999999999;
  dUpperRank = 0;
  for (i = 0; i < ddDescKeys.length; i++) {
    if (ddArray[ddDescKeys[i]] < dUpperPoint) {
      ddRank[ddDescKeys[i]] = i + 1;
      dUpperPoint = ddArray[ddDescKeys[i]];
      dUpperRank = ddRank[ddDescKeys[i]];
    } else {
      ddRank[ddDescKeys[i]] = dUpperRank;
    }
  }
  
  return ddRank;
}

function rightVisible(right_ul_id)
{
  var i;
  var right_li_id_first = right_ul_id + '_first';
  var right_ul          = document.getElementById(right_ul_id);
  var right_li_array    = right_ul.childNodes; 
  
  right_ul.style.backgroundColor = '#ffddbb';
  for (i = 1; i < right_li_array.length; i++) {
    right_li_array[i].style.display = 'block';
  }
}

function rightHidden(right_ul_id)
{
  var i;
  var right_li_id_first = right_ul_id + '_first';
  var right_ul          = document.getElementById(right_ul_id);
  var right_li_array    = right_ul.childNodes; 
  
  right_ul.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff';
  for (i = 1; i < right_li_array.length; i++) {
    right_li_array[i].style.display = 'none';
  }
}

function rewriteScore(sDdrcode, ddSinglePlay, ddDoublePlay, ddSingleCount, ddDoubleCount, dsSingleAverage, dsDoubleAverage,
                      dddSingleIndex, ddsSingleMusic, dddSingleSequence, ddsSingleScore, dddSingleFc, ddsSingleUpdate,
                      dddDoubleIndex, ddsDoubleMusic, dddDoubleSequence, ddsDoubleScore, dddDoubleFc, ddsDoubleUpdate)
{
  var sDivs, i;
  
  sDivs = '';
  for (i = 0; i < ddSinglePlay.length; i++) {
    if (1 <= ddSingleCount[i]) {
      sDivs += buildStyleDifficultyDiv(0, i, sDdrcode, ddSinglePlay[i], ddSingleCount[i], dsSingleAverage[i],
                                       dddSingleIndex[i], ddsSingleMusic[i], dddSingleSequence[i], ddsSingleScore[i], dddSingleFc[i], ddsSingleUpdate[i]);
    }
  }
  for (i = 0; i < ddDoublePlay.length; i++) {
    if (1 <= ddDoubleCount[i]) {
      sDivs += buildStyleDifficultyDiv(1, i, sDdrcode, ddDoublePlay[i], ddDoubleCount[i], dsDoubleAverage[i],
                                       dddDoubleIndex[i], ddsDoubleMusic[i], dddDoubleSequence[i], ddsDoubleScore[i], dddDoubleFc[i], ddsDoubleUpdate[i]);
    }
  }
  
  document.getElementById('score').innerHTML = sDivs;
  return;
}

function buildStyleDifficultyDiv(dStyle, i, sDdrcode, dPlay, dCount, sAverage,
                                 ddIndex, dsMusic, ddSequence, dsScore, ddFc, dsUpdate)
{
  var dDifficulty, sId, sDiv, j, sStyle, s_;
  
  sStyle = g['dsStyle'][dStyle];
  dDifficulty = i + 1;
  sId = sStyle + '_' + dDifficulty;
  s_ = 'score_' + dStyle + '_' + dDifficulty;
  
  sDiv = '<div>' +
           '<a name="' + sStyle + '_' + dDifficulty + '"></a>' +
           '<div style="padding: 5px 0;">                    ' +
             '<span class="changeDisplay styleDifficulty" onclick="changeDivDisplay(\'' + sId + '\')">' + sStyle + ' ' + dDifficulty + '</span>' +
             '<span style="font-size: 12pt;"> ( Play…' + dPlay + '/' + dCount + '　Average…' + sAverage + ' )</span>' +
           '</div>' +
           '<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="2" id="' + sStyle + '_' + dDifficulty + '" style="margin-bottom: 40px; display: none;">' +
             '<tr>' +
               '<th>index</th>' +
               '<th class="music">Music</th>' +
               '<th class="sequence">Sequence</th>' +
               '<th class="score">Score</th>' +
               '<th class="update">Update</th>' +
             '</tr>';
         
  for (j = 0; j < ddIndex.length; j++) {
    sDiv += buildScoreTr(ddIndex[j], dsMusic[j], ddSequence[j], dsScore[j], ddFc[j], dsUpdate[j], dStyle);
  }
         
  sDiv += '  </table>                                       ' +
          '</div>';

  return sDiv;
}

function buildScoreTr(dIndex, sMusic, dSequence, sScore, dFc, sUpdate, dStyle)
{
  var sTr;
  
  sTr = '<tr>' +
        '<td>' + dIndex + '</td>' +
        '<td class="music"><a class="text" href="music.php?index=' + dIndex + '">' + sMusic + '</a></td>' +
        '<td><a class="text ' + g['dsSequenceClass'][dSequence] + '" href="music.php?index=' + dIndex + '&style=' + dStyle + '&sequence=' + dSequence + '">' + g['dsSequence'][dSequence] + '</a></td>' +
        '<td class="' + g['dsFcClass'][dFc] + '">' + sScore + '</td>' +
        '<td>' + sUpdate + '</td>' +
        '</tr>';
  
  return sTr;
}

function changeDivDisplay(sDisplay)
{
  var dStyle, dDisplay, sId;
  
  // 開いている難易度を選んだらクローズ
  if (document.getElementById(sDisplay).style.display != 'none') {
    document.getElementById(sDisplay).style.display = 'none';
    return;
  }
  
  document.getElementById(sDisplay).style.display = '';
}

window.onload = function()
{
  document.title = g['sSystemName'] + ' ' + sName + ' Score';
  document.formName.ddrcode.value = sDdrcode;
  
  document.getElementById('breadcrumb').innerHTML = '<div class="breadcrumbLeft">' +
                                                    '<a href="./">' + g['sSystemName'] + '</a>' + ' &gt; ' +
                                                    '<a href="./dancer_profile.php?ddrcode=' + sDdrcode + '">' + sName + '</a>' + ' &gt; ' +
                                                    'Score' +
                                                    '</div>' +
                                                    '<div class="breadcrumbRight">' +
                                                      'Password <input type="password" name="password" value="" size="10" />　' +
                                                      '<input type="button" value="更新画面へ" onclick="document.formName.submit();" />' +
                                                    '</div>' +
                                                    '<div style="clear: both;"></div>' +
                                                    '<hr size="1" />';
                                                    
  document.getElementById('rightNavi').innerHTML = buildDancerRightNavi(sDdrcode);
  document.getElementById('right_difficulty_first').style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('right_series_first'    ).style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('right_initial_first'   ).style.display = 'block';
  
  rewriteScore(sDdrcode, ddSinglePlay, ddDoublePlay, ddSingleCount, ddDoubleCount, dsSingleAverage, dsDoubleAverage,
               dddSingleIndex, ddsSingleMusic, dddSingleSequence, ddsSingleScore, dddSingleFc, ddsSingleUpdate,
               dddDoubleIndex, ddsDoubleMusic, dddDoubleSequence, ddsDoubleScore, dddDoubleFc, ddsDoubleUpdate);
  if (sDisplay != '') {
    changeDivDisplay(sDisplay);
  }
  
  document.getElementById('footer').innerHTML = buildFooter(dNowYear);
  document.getElementById('process_time').innerHTML = buildProcessTime(dJavaScriptStart, sProcessTime);
}
